GT Equivalence Verification (PO22)
============================================================
GT: -c0*beta*v - beta*exp(-Abs(x))*v - mu*(c1 - x**c2)*v - omega0**c3*x**c4
Candidate formulas: 50

GT (fixed) simplifies to a specific form in variables \(x,v\) only:
\[
\text{GT}= -1.1598282332023\,x^3\;+\;0.752289977167006\,v\,x^2\;-\;1.366305954203476\,v\;-\;0.307007988518235\,v\,e^{-|x|}.
\]
So GT is **polynomial in \(x\)** except for the **non-polynomial term** \(v e^{-|x|}\). There is **no \(t\)** dependence, no trig, no rational-in-\(x\) factors, no \(v^3\), no \(|v|\), etc.

A candidate can only match if it can reproduce **exactly**:
- an \(x^3\) term (coefficient \(-1.1598...\)),
- a \(v x^2\) term (coefficient \(+0.7522899...\)),
- a \(v\) constant term (coefficient \(-1.3663059...\)),
- and crucially a \(v e^{-|x|}\) term (coefficient \(-0.3070079...\)),
possibly under a domain restriction like \(x\ge 0\) (then \(e^{-|x|}=e^{-x}\)) or \(x\le 0\) (then \(e^{-|x|}=e^{x}\)).

Now check candidates:

1. \(c_4 v\cos(c_5 x)\) cannot become \(v e^{-|x|}\) on any interval (cosine is oscillatory, exponential is monotone). No.

GT Equivalence Verification (PO22)
============================================================
GT: -c0*beta*v - beta*exp(-Abs(x))*v - mu*(c1 - x**c2)*v - omega0**c3*x**c4
Candidates evaluated: 50
Matched candidate IDs: []
Matched candidates: []

I need to compare each candidate against the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT numerical expression:** `-0.752289977167006*v*(1 - x**2) - 0.61401597703647*v - 0.307007988518235*v*exp(-Abs(x)) - 1.1598282332023*x**3`

Since x is strictly positive on this benchmark, `Abs(x) = x`, so:
`-0.752289977167006*v + 0.752289977167006*v*x**2 - 0.61401597703647*v - 0.307007988518235*v*exp(-x) - 1.1598282332023*x**3`

Combining v terms:
`-(0.752289977167006 + 0.61401597703647)*v + 0.752289977167006*v*x**2 - 0.307007988518235*v*exp(-x) - 1.1598282332023*x**3`
`= -1.366305954203476*v + 0.752289977167006*v*x**2 - 0.307007988518235*v*exp(-x) - 1.1598282332023*x**3`

The GT has these basis functions:
1. `v` (constant coefficient)
2. `v*x**2` 
3. `v*exp(-x)` 
4. `x**3`

This is critical: the term `v*exp(-x)` cannot be replicated by polynomial terms, trigonometric terms, or other non-exponential-decay terms. Any candidate that matches must contain a term equivalent to `v*exp(-x)`.

Let me check each candidate for the presence of `v*exp(-x)` or equivalent:

**Candidates with polynomial-only terms in x and v** (no exp(-x) possible):
- Candidates 3, 4, 5, 8, 13, 21, 25, 26, 29, 33, 37, 39, 42, 47: These only have polynomial terms in x and v. They CANNOT produce `v*exp(-x)`. **NO MATCH**

**Candidates with exp but wrong structure:**
- Candidate 9: has `exp(c8*v**2)` - not `exp(-x)`. **NO MATCH**

- Candidate 36: has `x**2*exp(c5*v)` - not `v*exp(-x)`. **NO MATCH**

**Candidates with trigonometric terms:** sin/cos cannot equal exp(-x). 
- Candidates 1, 2, 12, 16, 17, 23, 34, 41, 43, 45, 46, 50: These use trig functions but none can produce `v*exp(-x)`. **NO MATCH**

**Candidates with Max/Abs terms:** These piecewise functions cannot produce `v*exp(-x)`.
- Candidates 6, 7, 10, 14, 15, 20, 30, 31, 32, 35, 48, 49: **NO MATCH**

**Candidates with v*Abs(v) or v**3:** Cannot produce `v*exp(-x)`.
- Candidates 40: has `v*Abs(v)` and a power term. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 19:** Has `v/(c6 + Abs(v))` - not `v*exp(-x)`. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 22:** Has `x**c5*exp(c6*v)` and `cos(c8*t)`. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 28:** `c0*x*exp(c1*x) + c2*v*x**2 + c3*v + c4*x**3`. Has `x*exp(c1*x)` but not `v*exp(-x)`. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 38:** Has `x*exp(c1*x)` and `v**3` and `sin`. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 44:** Rational functions in x. Cannot produce `v*exp(-x)`. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 18:** Complex expression with `exp`, `cos`, `Abs`. The structure doesn't allow isolating `v*exp(-x)`. **NO MATCH**

After careful analysis, **none** of the candidates contain the essential `v*exp(-x)` term needed to match the GT.
